But our machine 
can't just go to the 
internet with its local IP.
Therefore, we use NAT

replaces source IP
with an IP of its own
choosing ^MmMrEphv

the needed PC

NOTE: 3 Way Handshake is needed
to know who is who!

It also prevents IP Spoofing ^q2Ousgn3

CDN ^loP9Jj6T

When files / images are uploaded to the server, 
they are uploaded to only one. Meaning they won't
be available in others

To prevent this we have CDNs.

Name of files are stored in DB, but the file itself is in
CDN storage ^ddBgUXeb
